ble\+\_\+device\+\_\+dead\+\_\+handler handler for B\+LE device dead indication handler. When the application receives

The callback pointers are registered according to the group type of B\+LE Events request is received \mbox{\hyperlink{at__ble__api_8h_a3324640b95f33169515f89738ed5baeba459fa57065ec575b1828a2381e373cc1}{A\+T\+\_\+\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+L\+E\+C\+B\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+N\+\_\+\+R\+EQ}}
